General #CEQA rule is that impacts of a project on the env. must be analyzed - Cal Sup Ct says there are limited exceptions to this rule
If a project might exacerbate env. hazards or falls w/in exceptions to the general rule impacts of env. on a project must be analyzed #CEQA
Cal Supreme Court rules that in certain limited cases the impacts of the environment on a project - #CEQA in reverse - must be analyzed
